# API

This is a guide of all facility API endpoints for KMHFR

import BrowserWindow from '../../../src/components/BrowserWindow'

### api facilities_contacts_list



> Code samples

```javascript

const headers = {
  'Accept':'application/json'
};

fetch('https://api.kmhfr.health.go.ke/api/facilities/contacts/',
{
  method: 'GET',

  headers: headers
})
.then(function(res) {
    return res.json();
}).then(function(body) {
    console.log(body);
});

```

`GET /api/facilities/contacts/`

*Lists and creates facility contacts*

facility -- A facility's pk
contact -- A contact's pk
Created --  Date the record was Created
Updated -- Date the record was Updated
Created_by -- User who created the record
Updated_by -- User who updated the record
active  -- Boolean is the record active
deleted -- Boolean is the record deleted

<h3 id="api_facilities_contacts_list-parameters">Parameters</h3>

|Name|In|Type|Required|Description|
|---|---|---|---|---|
|ordering|query|string|false|Which field to use when ordering the results.|
|page|query|integer|false|A page number within the paginated result set.|
|page_size|query|integer|false|Number of results to return per page.|

> Example responses

> 200 Response

<BrowserWindow>
```json
{
  "count": 0,
  "next": "http://example.com",
  "previous": "http://example.com",
  "results": [
    {
      "id": "497f6eca-6276-4993-bfeb-53cbbbba6f08",
      "contact_type": "string",
      "actual_contact": "string",
      "created": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
      "updated": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
      "deleted": true,
      "active": true,
      "search": "string",
      "created_by": 0,
      "updated_by": 0,
      "facility": "c7817696-f95c-43d7-adb1-358006544c72",
      "contact": "ad596931-5d7c-4d2b-907e-5b64c9432eb4"
    }
  ]
}
```
</BrowserWindow>



<h3 id="api_facilities_contacts_list-responses">Responses</h3>

|Status|Meaning|Description|Schema|
|---|---|---|---|
|200|[OK](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-6.3.1)|none|Inline|

<h3 id="api_facilities_contacts_list-responseschema">Response Schema</h3>

Status Code **200**

|Name|Type|Required|Restrictions|Description|
|---|---|---|---|---|
|» count|integer|true|none|none|
|» next|string(uri)¦null|false|none|none|
|» previous|string(uri)¦null|false|none|none|
|» results|[[FacilityContact](schema#facilitycontact)]|true|none|none|
|»» id|string(uuid)|false|read-only|none|
|»» contact_type|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» actual_contact|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» created|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»» updated|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»» deleted|boolean|false|none|none|
|»» active|boolean|false|none|Indicates whether the record has been retired?|
|»» search|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» created_by|integer|false|none|none|
|»» updated_by|integer|false|none|none|
|»» facility|string(uuid)|true|none|none|
|»» contact|string(uuid)|true|none|none|

:::note
To perform this operation, you must be authenticated by means of one of the following methods:
Basic
:::


### api facilities_contacts_create



> Code samples

```javascript
const inputBody = '{
  "created": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
  "updated": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
  "deleted": true,
  "active": true,
  "created_by": 0,
  "updated_by": 0,
  "facility": "c7817696-f95c-43d7-adb1-358006544c72",
  "contact": "ad596931-5d7c-4d2b-907e-5b64c9432eb4"
}';
const headers = {
  'Content-Type':'application/json',
  'Accept':'application/json'
};

fetch('https://api.kmhfr.health.go.ke/api/facilities/contacts/',
{
  method: 'POST',
  body: inputBody,
  headers: headers
})
.then(function(res) {
    return res.json();
}).then(function(body) {
    console.log(body);
});

```

`POST /api/facilities/contacts/`

*Lists and creates facility contacts*

facility -- A facility's pk
contact -- A contact's pk
Created --  Date the record was Created
Updated -- Date the record was Updated
Created_by -- User who created the record
Updated_by -- User who updated the record
active  -- Boolean is the record active
deleted -- Boolean is the record deleted

> Body parameter

<BrowserWindow>
```json
{
  "created": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
  "updated": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
  "deleted": true,
  "active": true,
  "created_by": 0,
  "updated_by": 0,
  "facility": "c7817696-f95c-43d7-adb1-358006544c72",
  "contact": "ad596931-5d7c-4d2b-907e-5b64c9432eb4"
}
```
</BrowserWindow>



<h3 id="api_facilities_contacts_create-parameters">Parameters</h3>

|Name|In|Type|Required|Description|
|---|---|---|---|---|
|body|body|[FacilityContact](schema#facilitycontact)|true|none|

> Example responses

> 201 Response

<BrowserWindow>
```json
{
  "id": "497f6eca-6276-4993-bfeb-53cbbbba6f08",
  "contact_type": "string",
  "actual_contact": "string",
  "created": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
  "updated": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
  "deleted": true,
  "active": true,
  "search": "string",
  "created_by": 0,
  "updated_by": 0,
  "facility": "c7817696-f95c-43d7-adb1-358006544c72",
  "contact": "ad596931-5d7c-4d2b-907e-5b64c9432eb4"
}
```
</BrowserWindow>



<h3 id="api_facilities_contacts_create-responses">Responses</h3>

|Status|Meaning|Description|Schema|
|---|---|---|---|
|201|[Created](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-6.3.2)|none|[FacilityContact](schema#facilitycontact)|

:::note
To perform this operation, you must be authenticated by means of one of the following methods:
Basic
:::

### api facilities_contacts_read



> Code samples

```javascript

const headers = {
  'Accept':'application/json'
};

fetch('https://api.kmhfr.health.go.ke/api/facilities/contacts/{id}/',
{
  method: 'GET',

  headers: headers
})
.then(function(res) {
    return res.json();
}).then(function(body) {
    console.log(body);
});

```

`GET /api/facilities/contacts/{id}/`

Retrieves a particular facility contact

<h3 id="api_facilities_contacts_read-parameters">Parameters</h3>

|Name|In|Type|Required|Description|
|---|---|---|---|---|
|id|path|string(uuid)|true|A UUID string identifying this facility contact.|

> Example responses

> 200 Response

<BrowserWindow>
```json
{
  "id": "497f6eca-6276-4993-bfeb-53cbbbba6f08",
  "contact_type": "string",
  "actual_contact": "string",
  "created": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
  "updated": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
  "deleted": true,
  "active": true,
  "search": "string",
  "created_by": 0,
  "updated_by": 0,
  "facility": "c7817696-f95c-43d7-adb1-358006544c72",
  "contact": "ad596931-5d7c-4d2b-907e-5b64c9432eb4"
}
```
</BrowserWindow>



<h3 id="api_facilities_contacts_read-responses">Responses</h3>

|Status|Meaning|Description|Schema|
|---|---|---|---|
|200|[OK](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-6.3.1)|none|[FacilityContact](schema#facilitycontact)|

:::note
To perform this operation, you must be authenticated by means of one of the following methods:
Basic
:::

### api facilities_contacts_update



> Code samples

```javascript
const inputBody = '{
  "created": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
  "updated": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
  "deleted": true,
  "active": true,
  "created_by": 0,
  "updated_by": 0,
  "facility": "c7817696-f95c-43d7-adb1-358006544c72",
  "contact": "ad596931-5d7c-4d2b-907e-5b64c9432eb4"
}';
const headers = {
  'Content-Type':'application/json',
  'Accept':'application/json'
};

fetch('https://api.kmhfr.health.go.ke/api/facilities/contacts/{id}/',
{
  method: 'PUT',
  body: inputBody,
  headers: headers
})
.then(function(res) {
    return res.json();
}).then(function(body) {
    console.log(body);
});

```

### api facilities_contacts_partial_update



> Code samples

```javascript
const inputBody = '{
  "created": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
  "updated": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
  "deleted": true,
  "active": true,
  "created_by": 0,
  "updated_by": 0,
  "facility": "c7817696-f95c-43d7-adb1-358006544c72",
  "contact": "ad596931-5d7c-4d2b-907e-5b64c9432eb4"
}';
const headers = {
  'Content-Type':'application/json',
  'Accept':'application/json'
};

fetch('https://api.kmhfr.health.go.ke/api/facilities/contacts/{id}/',
{
  method: 'PATCH',
  body: inputBody,
  headers: headers
})
.then(function(res) {
    return res.json();
}).then(function(body) {
    console.log(body);
});

```

### api facilities_facilities_list



> Code samples

```javascript

const headers = {
  'Accept':'application/json'
};

fetch('https://api.kmhfr.health.go.ke/api/facilities/facilities/',
{
  method: 'GET',

  headers: headers
})
.then(function(res) {
    return res.json();
}).then(function(body) {
    console.log(body);
});

```

`GET /api/facilities/facilities/`

*Lists and creates facilities*

name -- The name of the facility<br/>
code -- A list of comma separated facility codes (one or more)<br/>
description -- The description of the facility<br/>
facility_type -- A list of comma separated facility type's pk<br/>
operation_status -- A list of comma separated operation statuses pks<br/>
ward -- A list of comma separated ward pks (one or more)<br/>
ward_code -- A list of comma separated ward codes<br/>
county_code -- A list of comma separated county codes<br/>
constituency_code -- A list of comma separated constituency codes<br/>
county -- A list of comma separated county pks<br/>
constituency -- A list of comma separated constituency pks<br/>
owner -- A list of comma separated owner pks<br/>
number_of_inpatient_beds -- A list of comma separated integers<br/>
number_of_beds -- A list of comma separated integers<br/>
number_of_cots -- A list of comma separated integers<br/>
open_whole_day -- Boolean True/False<br/>
is_classified -- Boolean True/False<br/>
is_published -- Boolean True/False<br/>
is_regulated -- Boolean True/False<br/>
service_category -- A service category's pk<br/>
Created --  Date the record was Created<br/>
Updated -- Date the record was Updated<br/>
Created_by -- User who created the record<br/>
Updated_by -- User who updated the record<br/>
active  -- Boolean is the record active<br/>
deleted -- Boolean is the record deleted<br/>

<h3 id="api_facilities_facilities_list-parameters">Parameters</h3>

|Name|In|Type|Required|Description|
|---|---|---|---|---|
|ordering|query|string|false|Which field to use when ordering the results.|
|page|query|integer|false|A page number within the paginated result set.|
|page_size|query|integer|false|Number of results to return per page.|

> Example responses

> 200 Response

`POST /api/facilities/facilities/`

*Lists and creates facilities*

name -- The name of the facility<br/>
code -- A list of comma separated facility codes (one or more)<br/>
description -- The description of the facility<br/>
facility_type -- A list of comma separated facility type's pk<br/>
operation_status -- A list of comma separated operation statuses pks<br/>
ward -- A list of comma separated ward pks (one or more)<br/>
ward_code -- A list of comma separated ward codes<br/>
county_code -- A list of comma separated county codes<br/>
constituency_code -- A list of comma separated constituency codes<br/>
county -- A list of comma separated county pks<br/>
constituency -- A list of comma separated constituency pks<br/>
owner -- A list of comma separated owner pks<br/>
number_of_inpatient_beds -- A list of comma separated integers<br/>
number_of_beds -- A list of comma separated integers<br/>
number_of_cots -- A list of comma separated integers<br/>
open_whole_day -- Boolean True/False<br/>
is_classified -- Boolean True/False<br/>
is_published -- Boolean True/False<br/>
is_regulated -- Boolean True/False<br/>
service_category -- A service category's pk<br/>
Created --  Date the record was Created<br/>
Updated -- Date the record was Updated<br/>
Created_by -- User who created the record<br/>
Updated_by -- User who updated the record<br/>
active  -- Boolean is the record active<br/>
deleted -- Boolean is the record deleted<br/>

> Body parameter

:::

### api facilities_facilities_read



> Code samples

```javascript

const headers = {
  'Accept':'application/json'
};

fetch('https://api.kmhfr.health.go.ke/api/facilities/facilities/{id}/',
{
  method: 'GET',

  headers: headers
})
.then(function(res) {
    return res.json();
}).then(function(body) {
    console.log(body);
});

```

`GET /api/facilities/facilities/{id}/`

Retrieves a particular facility

<h3 id="api_facilities_facilities_read-parameters">Parameters</h3>

|Name|In|Type|Required|Description|
|---|---|---|---|---|
|id|path|string(uuid)|true|A UUID string identifying this facility.|

```json
    {
      "created": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",

      "active": true,
```

`GET /api/facilities/facility_admission_status/`

*Lists and creates facility admission statuses*

Created --  Date the record was Created
Updated -- Date the record was Updated
Created_by -- User who created the record
Updated_by -- User who updated the record
active  -- Boolean is the record active
deleted -- Boolean is the record deleted

<h3 id="api_facilities_facility_admission_status_list-parameters">Parameters</h3>

|Name|In|Type|Required|Description|
|---|---|---|---|---|
|ordering|query|string|false|Which field to use when ordering the results.|
|page|query|integer|false|A page number within the paginated result set.|
|page_size|query|integer|false|Number of results to return per page.|

> Example responses

> 200 Response

<BrowserWindow>
```json
{
  "count": 0,
  "next": "http://example.com",
  "previous": "http://example.com",
  "results": [
    {
      "id": "497f6eca-6276-4993-bfeb-53cbbbba6f08",
      "created": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
      "updated": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
      "deleted": true,
      "active": true,
      "search": "string",
      "name": "string",
      "description": "string",
      "created_by": 0,
      "updated_by": 0
    }
  ]
}
```
</BrowserWindow>



<h3 id="api_facilities_facility_admission_status_list-responses">Responses</h3>

|Status|Meaning|Description|Schema|
|---|---|---|---|
|200|[OK](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-6.3.1)|none|Inline|

<h3 id="api_facilities_facility_admission_status_list-responseschema">Response Schema</h3>

Status Code **200**

|Name|Type|Required|Restrictions|Description|
|---|---|---|---|---|
|» count|integer|true|none|none|
|» next|string(uri)¦null|false|none|none|
|» previous|string(uri)¦null|false|none|none|
|» results|[[FacilityAdmissionStatus](schema#facilityadmissionstatus)]|true|none|none|
|»» id|string(uuid)|false|read-only|none|
|»» created|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»» updated|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»» deleted|boolean|false|none|none|
|»» active|boolean|false|none|Indicates whether the record has been retired?|
|»» search|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» name|string|true|none|A short name representing the admission status e.g NOT ADMITTING|
|»» description|string¦null|false|none|A short explanation of what the admission status entails.|
|»» created_by|integer|false|none|none|
|»» updated_by|integer|false|none|none|

:::note
To perform this operation, you must be authenticated by means of one of the following methods:
Basic
:::

`GET /api/facilities/facility_depts/`

*Lists and creates facility departments*

created ---  Date the record was created
updated -- Date the record was updated
created_by -- User who created the record
updated_by -- User who updated the record
active  -- Boolean is the record active
deleted -- Boolean is the record deleted

<h3 id="api_facilities_facility_depts_list-parameters">Parameters</h3>

|Name|In|Type|Required|Description|
|---|---|---|---|---|
|ordering|query|string|false|Which field to use when ordering the results.|
|page|query|integer|false|A page number within the paginated result set.|
|page_size|query|integer|false|Number of results to return per page.|

> Example responses

> 200 Response

<BrowserWindow>
```json
{
  "count": 0,
  "next": "http://example.com",
  "previous": "http://example.com",
  "results": [
    {
      "id": "497f6eca-6276-4993-bfeb-53cbbbba6f08",
      "regulatory_body_name": "string",
      "created": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
      "updated": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
      "deleted": true,
      "active": true,
      "search": "string",
      "name": "string",
      "description": "string",
      "created_by": 0,
      "updated_by": 0,
      "regulatory_body": "5cc1a352-328e-4e0a-b0cc-f1e5c296e6ec"
    }
  ]
}
```
</BrowserWindow>



<h3 id="api_facilities_facility_depts_list-responses">Responses</h3>

|Status|Meaning|Description|Schema|
|---|---|---|---|
|200|[OK](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-6.3.1)|none|Inline|

<h3 id="api_facilities_facility_depts_list-responseschema">Response Schema</h3>

Status Code **200**

|Name|Type|Required|Restrictions|Description|
|---|---|---|---|---|
|» count|integer|true|none|none|
|» next|string(uri)¦null|false|none|none|
|» previous|string(uri)¦null|false|none|none|
|» results|[[FacilityDepartment](schema#facilitydepartment)]|true|none|none|
|»» id|string(uuid)|false|read-only|none|
|»» regulatory_body_name|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» created|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»» updated|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»» deleted|boolean|false|none|none|
|»» active|boolean|false|none|Indicates whether the record has been retired?|
|»» search|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» name|string|true|none|none|
|»» description|string¦null|false|none|none|
|»» created_by|integer|false|none|none|

### api facilities_facility_depts_partial_update



> Code samples

```javascript
const inputBody = '{
  "created": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
  "updated": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
  "deleted": true,
  "active": true,
  "name": "string",
  "description": "string",
  "created_by": 0,
  "updated_by": 0,
  "regulatory_body": "5cc1a352-328e-4e0a-b0cc-f1e5c296e6ec"
}';
const headers = {
  'Content-Type':'application/json',
  'Accept':'application/json'
};

fetch('https://api.kmhfr.health.go.ke/api/facilities/facility_depts/{id}/',
{
  method: 'PATCH',
  body: inputBody,
  headers: headers
})
.then(function(res) {
```

`GET /api/facilities/facility_infrastructure/`

*Lists and creates links between facilities and infrastructure.*

facility -- A facility's pk
Created --  Date the record was Created
Updated -- Date the record was Updated
Created_by -- User who created the record
Updated_by -- User who updated the record
active  -- Boolean is the record active
deleted -- Boolean is the record deleted

<h3 id="api_facilities_facility_infrastructure_list-parameters">Parameters</h3>

|Name|In|Type|Required|Description|
|---|---|---|---|---|
|ordering|query|string|false|Which field to use when ordering the results.|
|page|query|integer|false|A page number within the paginated result set.|
|page_size|query|integer|false|Number of results to return per page.|

> Example responses

> 200 Response

<BrowserWindow>
```json
{
  "count": 0,
  "next": "http://example.com",
  "previous": "http://example.com",
  "results": [
    {
      "id": "497f6eca-6276-4993-bfeb-53cbbbba6f08",
      "infrastructure_name": "string",
      "option_display_value": "string",
      "created": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
      "updated": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
      "deleted": true,
      "active": true,
      "search": "string",
      "count": -2147483648,
      "present": true,
      "created_by": 0,
      "updated_by": 0,
      "facility": "c7817696-f95c-43d7-adb1-358006544c72",
      "infrastructure": "1d1f492c-f2d6-4e1d-bc79-8be05af7e78c"
    }
  ]
}
```
</BrowserWindow>



<h3 id="api_facilities_facility_infrastructure_list-responses">Responses</h3>

|Status|Meaning|Description|Schema|
|---|---|---|---|
|200|[OK](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-6.3.1)|none|Inline|

<h3 id="api_facilities_facility_infrastructure_list-responseschema">Response Schema</h3>

Status Code **200**

|Name|Type|Required|Restrictions|Description|
|---|---|---|---|---|
|» count|integer|true|none|none|
|» next|string(uri)¦null|false|none|none|
|» previous|string(uri)¦null|false|none|none|
|» results|[[FacilityInfrastructure](schema#facilityinfrastructure)]|true|none|none|
|»» id|string(uuid)|false|read-only|none|
|»» infrastructure_name|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» option_display_value|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» created|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»» updated|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»» deleted|boolean|false|none|none|
|»» active|boolean|false|none|Indicates whether the record has been retired?|
|»» search|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» count|integer|false|none|The actual number of infrastructure items in a facility.|
|»» present|boolean|false|none|True if the listed infrastructure is present.|
|»» created_by|integer|false|none|none|
|»» updated_by|integer|false|none|none|
|»» facility|string(uuid)|true|none|none|
|»» infrastructure|string(uuid)|true|none|none|

:::note
To perform this operation, you must be authenticated by means of one of the following methods:
Basic
:::

<h3 id="api_facilities_facility_infrastructure_delete-parameters">Parameters</h3>

|Name|In|Type|Required|Description|
|---|---|---|---|---|
|id|path|string(uuid)|true|A UUID string identifying this facility infrastructure.|

<h3 id="api_facilities_facility_infrastructure_delete-responses">Responses</h3>

|Status|Meaning|Description|Schema|
|---|---|---|---|
|204|[No Content](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-6.3.5)|none|None|

:::note
To perform this operation, you must be authenticated by means of one of the following methods:
Basic
:::

`GET /api/facilities/facility_operation_state/`

*Lists and creates operation statuses for facilities*

Created ---  Date the record was Created
Updated -- Date the record was Updated
Created_by -- User who created the record
Updated_by -- User who updated the record
active  -- Boolean is the record active
deleted -- Boolean is the record deleted

<h3 id="api_facilities_facility_operation_state_list-parameters">Parameters</h3>

|Name|In|Type|Required|Description|
|---|---|---|---|---|
|ordering|query|string|false|Which field to use when ordering the results.|
|page|query|integer|false|A page number within the paginated result set.|
|page_size|query|integer|false|Number of results to return per page.|

> Example responses

> 200 Response

<BrowserWindow>
```json
{
  "count": 0,
  "next": "http://example.com",
  "previous": "http://example.com",
  "results": [
    {
      "id": "497f6eca-6276-4993-bfeb-53cbbbba6f08",
      "created": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
      "updated": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
      "deleted": true,
      "active": true,
      "search": "string",
      "reason": "string",
      "created_by": 0,
      "updated_by": 0,
```

facility -- A facility's pk

Updated -- Date the record was Updated

Updated_by -- User who updated the record
active  -- Boolean is the record active
deleted -- Boolean is the record deleted

`GET /api/facilities/facility_services/`

*Lists and creates links between facilities and services*

facility -- A facility's pk
selected_option -- A service selected_option's pk
Created --  Date the record was Created
Updated -- Date the record was Updated
Created_by -- User who created the record
Updated_by -- User who updated the record
active  -- Boolean is the record active
deleted -- Boolean is the record deleted

<h3 id="api_facilities_facility_services_list-parameters">Parameters</h3>

|Name|In|Type|Required|Description|
|---|---|---|---|---|
|ordering|query|string|false|Which field to use when ordering the results.|
|page|query|integer|false|A page number within the paginated result set.|
|page_size|query|integer|false|Number of results to return per page.|

> Example responses

> 200 Response

<BrowserWindow>
```json
{
  "count": 0,
  "next": "http://example.com",
  "previous": "http://example.com",
  "results": [
    {
      "id": "497f6eca-6276-4993-bfeb-53cbbbba6f08",
      "service_name": "string",
      "service_code": "string",
      "option_display_value": "string",
      "average_rating": "string",
      "number_of_ratings": "string",
      "service_has_options": "string",
      "created": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
      "updated": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
      "deleted": true,
      "active": true,
      "search": "string",
      "is_confirmed": true,
      "is_cancelled": true,
      "created_by": 0,
      "updated_by": 0,
      "facility": "c7817696-f95c-43d7-adb1-358006544c72",
      "option": "e7c2432c-b004-45c5-a282-bcaf6d903541",
      "service": "cd8c5e52-093e-43db-9c42-184f00e681dd"
    }
  ]
}
```
</BrowserWindow>



<h3 id="api_facilities_facility_services_list-responses">Responses</h3>

|Status|Meaning|Description|Schema|
|---|---|---|---|
|200|[OK](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-6.3.1)|none|Inline|

<h3 id="api_facilities_facility_services_list-responseschema">Response Schema</h3>

Status Code **200**

|Name|Type|Required|Restrictions|Description|
|---|---|---|---|---|
|» count|integer|true|none|none|
|» next|string(uri)¦null|false|none|none|
|» previous|string(uri)¦null|false|none|none|
|» results|[[FacilityService](schema#facilityservice)]|true|none|none|
|»» id|string(uuid)|false|read-only|none|
|»» service_name|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» service_code|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» option_display_value|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» average_rating|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» number_of_ratings|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» service_has_options|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» created|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»» updated|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»» deleted|boolean|false|none|none|
|»» active|boolean|false|none|Indicates whether the record has been retired?|
|»» search|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» is_confirmed|boolean|false|none|Indicates whether a service has been approved by the CHRIO|
|»» is_cancelled|boolean|false|none|Indicates whether a service has been canceled by the CHRIO|
|»» created_by|integer|false|none|none|
|»» updated_by|integer|false|none|none|
|»» facility|string(uuid)|true|none|none|
|»» option|string(uuid)¦null|false|none|none|
|»» service|string(uuid)|true|none|none|

:::note
To perform this operation, you must be authenticated by means of one of the following methods:
Basic
:::

`GET /api/facilities/facility_status/`

*Lists and creates facility operation statuses*

Created --  Date the record was Created
Updated -- Date the record was Updated
Created_by -- User who created the record
Updated_by -- User who updated the record
active  -- Boolean is the record active
deleted -- Boolean is the record deleted

<h3 id="api_facilities_facility_status_list-parameters">Parameters</h3>

|Name|In|Type|Required|Description|
|---|---|---|---|---|
|ordering|query|string|false|Which field to use when ordering the results.|
|page|query|integer|false|A page number within the paginated result set.|
|page_size|query|integer|false|Number of results to return per page.|

> Example responses

> 200 Response

<BrowserWindow>
```json
{
  "count": 0,
  "next": "http://example.com",
  "previous": "http://example.com",
  "results": [
    {
      "id": "497f6eca-6276-4993-bfeb-53cbbbba6f08",
      "created": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
      "updated": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
      "deleted": true,
      "active": true,
      "search": "string",
      "name": "string",
      "description": "string",
      "is_public_visible": true,
      "created_by": 0,
      "updated_by": 0
    }
  ]
}
```
</BrowserWindow>



<h3 id="api_facilities_facility_status_list-responses">Responses</h3>

|Status|Meaning|Description|Schema|
|---|---|---|---|
|200|[OK](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-6.3.1)|none|Inline|

<h3 id="api_facilities_facility_status_list-responseschema">Response Schema</h3>

Status Code **200**

|Name|Type|Required|Restrictions|Description|
|---|---|---|---|---|
|» count|integer|true|none|none|
|» next|string(uri)¦null|false|none|none|
|» previous|string(uri)¦null|false|none|none|
|» results|[[FacilityStatus](schema#facilitystatus)]|true|none|none|
|»» id|string(uuid)|false|read-only|none|
|»» created|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»» updated|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»» deleted|boolean|false|none|none|
|»» active|boolean|false|none|Indicates whether the record has been retired?|
|»» search|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» name|string|true|none|A short name representing the operation status e.g OPERATIONAL|
|»» description|string¦null|false|none|A short explanation of what the status entails.|
|»» is_public_visible|boolean|false|none|The facilities with this status should be visible to the public|
|»» created_by|integer|false|none|none|
|»» updated_by|integer|false|none|none|

:::note
To perform this operation, you must be authenticated by means of one of the following methods:
Basic
:::

`GET /api/facilities/facility_types_details/`

Lists and creates facility types
name -- Name of a facility type
sub_division -- A sub-division in a facility type
Created --  Date the record was Created
Updated -- Date the record was Updated
Created_by -- User who created the record
Updated_by -- User who updated the record
active  -- Boolean is the record active
deleted -- Boolean is the record deleted

<h3 id="api_facilities_facility_types_details_list-parameters">Parameters</h3>

|Name|In|Type|Required|Description|
|---|---|---|---|---|
|ordering|query|string|false|Which field to use when ordering the results.|
|page|query|integer|false|A page number within the paginated result set.|
|page_size|query|integer|false|Number of results to return per page.|

> Example responses

> 200 Response

<BrowserWindow>
```json
{
  "count": 0,
  "next": "http://example.com",
  "previous": "http://example.com",
  "results": [
    {
      "id": "497f6eca-6276-4993-bfeb-53cbbbba6f08",
      "owner_type_name": "string",
      "created": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
      "updated": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
      "deleted": true,
      "active": true,
      "search": "string",
      "name": "string",
      "abbreviation": "string",
      "sub_division": "string",
      "created_by": 0,
      "updated_by": 0,
      "owner_type": "2c36d811-befc-4f66-ac99-1f27e70bdb0b",
      "preceding": "39541667-be02-4a84-8264-8868234629da",
      "parent": "42e2bc1b-6741-4e2e-b138-97b4a342c999"
    }
  ]
}
```
</BrowserWindow>



<h3 id="api_facilities_facility_types_details_list-responses">Responses</h3>

|Status|Meaning|Description|Schema|
|---|---|---|---|
|200|[OK](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-6.3.1)|none|Inline|

<h3 id="api_facilities_facility_types_details_list-responseschema">Response Schema</h3>

Status Code **200**

|Name|Type|Required|Restrictions|Description|
|---|---|---|---|---|
|» count|integer|true|none|none|
|» next|string(uri)¦null|false|none|none|
|» previous|string(uri)¦null|false|none|none|
|» results|[[FacilityType](schema#facilitytype)]|true|none|none|
|»» id|string(uuid)|false|read-only|none|
|»» owner_type_name|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» created|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»» updated|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»» deleted|boolean|false|none|none|
|»» active|boolean|false|none|Indicates whether the record has been retired?|
|»» search|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» name|string|true|none|A short unique name for the facility type e.g DISPENSARY|
|»» abbreviation|string¦null|false|none|none|
|»» sub_division|string¦null|false|none|Parent of the facility type e.g sub-district hospitals are under Hospitals.|
|»» created_by|integer|false|none|none|
|»» updated_by|integer|false|none|none|
|»» owner_type|string(uuid)¦null|false|none|none|
|»» preceding|string(uuid)¦null|false|none|The facility type that comes before this type|
|»» parent|string(uuid)¦null|false|none|none|

:::note
To perform this operation, you must be authenticated by means of one of the following methods:
Basic
:::

`GET /api/facilities/facility_units/`

*Lists and creates facility units*

facility -- A facility's pk
name -- Name of a facility unit
description -- Description of a facility unit
Created --  Date the record was Created
Updated -- Date the record was Updated
Created_by -- User who created the record
Updated_by -- User who updated the record
active  -- Boolean is the record active
deleted -- Boolean is the record deleted

<h3 id="api_facilities_facility_units_list-parameters">Parameters</h3>

|Name|In|Type|Required|Description|
|---|---|---|---|---|
|ordering|query|string|false|Which field to use when ordering the results.|
|page|query|integer|false|A page number within the paginated result set.|
|page_size|query|integer|false|Number of results to return per page.|

> Example responses

> 200 Response

<BrowserWindow>
```json
{
  "count": 0,
  "next": "http://example.com",
  "previous": "http://example.com",
  "results": [
    {
      "id": "497f6eca-6276-4993-bfeb-53cbbbba6f08",
      "regulation_status": "string",
      "unit_name": "string",
      "regulating_body_name": "string",
      "created": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
      "updated": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
      "deleted": true,
      "active": true,
      "search": "string",
      "license_number": "string",
      "registration_number": "string",
      "created_by": 0,
      "updated_by": 0,
      "facility": "c7817696-f95c-43d7-adb1-358006544c72",
      "unit": "96a6aa1e-fb68-45e6-a443-0913abfa47dd"
    }
  ]
}
```
</BrowserWindow>



<h3 id="api_facilities_facility_units_list-responses">Responses</h3>

|Status|Meaning|Description|Schema|
|---|---|---|---|
|200|[OK](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-6.3.1)|none|Inline|

<h3 id="api_facilities_facility_units_list-responseschema">Response Schema</h3>

Status Code **200**

|Name|Type|Required|Restrictions|Description|
|---|---|---|---|---|
|» count|integer|true|none|none|
|» next|string(uri)¦null|false|none|none|
|» previous|string(uri)¦null|false|none|none|
|» results|[[FacilityUnit](schema#facilityunit)]|true|none|none|
|»» id|string(uuid)|false|read-only|none|
|»» regulation_status|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» unit_name|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» regulating_body_name|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» created|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»» updated|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»» deleted|boolean|false|none|none|
|»» active|boolean|false|none|Indicates whether the record has been retired?|
|»» search|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» license_number|string¦null|false|none|none|
|»» registration_number|string¦null|false|none|none|
|»» created_by|integer|false|none|none|
|»» updated_by|integer|false|none|none|
|»» facility|string(uuid)|true|none|none|
|»» unit|string(uuid)|true|none|none|

:::note
To perform this operation, you must be authenticated by means of one of the following methods:
Basic
:::

### api facilities_facility_units_delete



> Code samples

```javascript

fetch('https://api.kmhfr.health.go.ke/api/facilities/facility_units/{id}/',
{
  method: 'DELETE'

})
.then(function(res) {
    return res.json();
```

Updated_by -- User who updated the record
active  -- Boolean is the record active
deleted -- Boolean is the record deleted

`GET /api/facilities/infrastructure/`

*Lists and creates infrastructure.*

category -- Infrastructure category pk
Created --  Date the record was Created
Updated -- Date the record was Updated
Created_by -- User who created the record
Updated_by -- User who updated the record
active  -- Boolean is the record active
deleted -- Boolean is the record deleted

<h3 id="api_facilities_infrastructure_list-parameters">Parameters</h3>

|Name|In|Type|Required|Description|
|---|---|---|---|---|
|ordering|query|string|false|Which field to use when ordering the results.|
|page|query|integer|false|A page number within the paginated result set.|
|page_size|query|integer|false|Number of results to return per page.|

> Example responses

> 200 Response

<BrowserWindow>
```json
{
  "count": 0,
  "next": "http://example.com",
  "previous": "http://example.com",
  "results": [
    {
      "id": "497f6eca-6276-4993-bfeb-53cbbbba6f08",
      "category_name": "string",
      "created": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
      "updated": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
      "deleted": true,
      "active": true,
      "search": "string",
      "name": "string",
      "description": "string",
      "abbreviation": "string",
      "numbers": true,
      "code": "string",
      "created_by": 0,
      "updated_by": 0,
      "category": "86d23d13-9dbb-46f3-82d0-25253c7750c3"
    }
  ]
}
```
</BrowserWindow>



<h3 id="api_facilities_infrastructure_list-responses">Responses</h3>

|Status|Meaning|Description|Schema|
|---|---|---|---|
|200|[OK](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-6.3.1)|none|Inline|

<h3 id="api_facilities_infrastructure_list-responseschema">Response Schema</h3>

Status Code **200**

|Name|Type|Required|Restrictions|Description|
|---|---|---|---|---|
|» count|integer|true|none|none|
|» next|string(uri)¦null|false|none|none|
|» previous|string(uri)¦null|false|none|none|
|» results|[[Infrastructure](schema#infrastructure)]|true|none|none|
|»» id|string(uuid)|false|read-only|none|
|»» category_name|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» created|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»» updated|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»» deleted|boolean|false|none|none|
|»» active|boolean|false|none|Indicates whether the record has been retired?|
|»» search|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» name|string|true|none|none|
|»» description|string¦null|false|none|none|
|»» abbreviation|string¦null|false|none|A short form for the infrastructure|
|»» numbers|boolean¦null|false|none|A flag to indicate whether an infrastructure item can have count/numbers tracked|
|»» code|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» created_by|integer|false|none|none|
|»» updated_by|integer|false|none|none|
|»» category|string(uuid)|true|none|The classification that the infrastructure item lies in.|

:::note
To perform this operation, you must be authenticated by means of one of the following methods:
Basic
:::

`GET /api/facilities/infrastructure_categories/`

*Lists and creates service categories.*

Created ---  Date the record was Created
Updated -- Date the record was Updated
Created_by -- User who created the record
Updated_by -- User who updated the record
active  -- Boolean is the record active
deleted -- Boolean is the record deleted

<h3 id="api_facilities_infrastructure_categories_list-parameters">Parameters</h3>

|Name|In|Type|Required|Description|
|---|---|---|---|---|
|ordering|query|string|false|Which field to use when ordering the results.|
|page|query|integer|false|A page number within the paginated result set.|
|page_size|query|integer|false|Number of results to return per page.|

> Example responses

> 200 Response

<BrowserWindow>
```json
{
  "count": 0,
  "next": "http://example.com",
  "previous": "http://example.com",
  "results": [
    {
      "id": "497f6eca-6276-4993-bfeb-53cbbbba6f08",
      "created": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
      "updated": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
      "deleted": true,
      "active": true,
      "search": "string",
      "name": "string",
      "description": "string",
      "abbreviation": "string",
      "created_by": 0,
      "updated_by": 0,
      "parent": "42e2bc1b-6741-4e2e-b138-97b4a342c999"
    }
  ]
}
```
</BrowserWindow>



<h3 id="api_facilities_infrastructure_categories_list-responses">Responses</h3>

|Status|Meaning|Description|Schema|
|---|---|---|---|
|200|[OK](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-6.3.1)|none|Inline|

<h3 id="api_facilities_infrastructure_categories_list-responseschema">Response Schema</h3>

Status Code **200**

|Name|Type|Required|Restrictions|Description|
|---|---|---|---|---|
|» count|integer|true|none|none|
|» next|string(uri)¦null|false|none|none|
|» previous|string(uri)¦null|false|none|none|
|» results|[[InfrastructureCategory](schema#infrastructurecategory)]|true|none|none|
|»» id|string(uuid)|false|read-only|none|
|»» created|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»» updated|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»» deleted|boolean|false|none|none|
|»» active|boolean|false|none|Indicates whether the record has been retired?|
|»» search|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» name|string|true|none|What is the name of the category?|
|»» description|string¦null|false|none|none|
|»» abbreviation|string¦null|false|none|A short form of the category e.g ANC for antenatal|
|»» created_by|integer|false|none|none|
|»» updated_by|integer|false|none|none|
|»» parent|string(uuid)¦null|false|none|The parent category under which the category falls|

:::note
To perform this operation, you must be authenticated by means of one of the following methods:
Basic
:::

`GET /api/facilities/keph/`

Lists and creates the  Kenya Essential Package for health (KEPH)
name -- Name of a level 1
description -- Description the KEPH
Created --  Date the record was Created
Updated -- Date the record was Updated
Created_by -- User who created the record
Updated_by -- User who updated the record
active  -- Boolean is the record active
deleted -- Boolean is the record deleted

<h3 id="api_facilities_keph_list-parameters">Parameters</h3>

|Name|In|Type|Required|Description|
|---|---|---|---|---|
|ordering|query|string|false|Which field to use when ordering the results.|
|page|query|integer|false|A page number within the paginated result set.|
|page_size|query|integer|false|Number of results to return per page.|

> Example responses

> 200 Response

<BrowserWindow>
```json
{
  "count": 0,
  "next": "http://example.com",
  "previous": "http://example.com",
  "results": [
    {
      "id": "497f6eca-6276-4993-bfeb-53cbbbba6f08",
      "created": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
      "updated": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
      "deleted": true,
      "active": true,
      "search": "string",
      "name": "string",
      "description": "string",
      "is_facility_level": true,
      "created_by": 0,
      "updated_by": 0
    }
  ]
}
```
</BrowserWindow>



<h3 id="api_facilities_keph_list-responses">Responses</h3>

|Status|Meaning|Description|Schema|
|---|---|---|---|
|200|[OK](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-6.3.1)|none|Inline|

<h3 id="api_facilities_keph_list-responseschema">Response Schema</h3>

Status Code **200**

|Name|Type|Required|Restrictions|Description|
|---|---|---|---|---|
|» count|integer|true|none|none|
|» next|string(uri)¦null|false|none|none|
|» previous|string(uri)¦null|false|none|none|
|» results|[[KephLevel](schema#kephlevel)]|true|none|none|
|»» id|string(uuid)|false|read-only|none|
|»» created|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»» updated|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»» deleted|boolean|false|none|none|
|»» active|boolean|false|none|Indicates whether the record has been retired?|
|»» search|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» name|string|true|none|The name of the KEPH e.g Level 1|
|»» description|string¦null|false|none|A short description of the KEPH level|
|»» is_facility_level|boolean|false|none|Is the KEPH level applicable to facilities|
|»» created_by|integer|false|none|none|
|»» updated_by|integer|false|none|none|

:::note
To perform this operation, you must be authenticated by means of one of the following methods:
Basic
:::

### api facilities_level_change_reasons_create

```javascript

  'Content-Type':'application/json',
  'Accept':'application/json'

  method: 'POST',

  headers: headers
})
.then(function(res) {
    return res.json();
```

```javascript
  "updated": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
  "deleted": true,
  "active": true,
  "created_by": 0,
  "updated_by": 0,
  "officer": "8481ed7f-8db9-4614-a252-b14694bf5ad4",
  "contact": "ad596931-5d7c-4d2b-907e-5b64c9432eb4"
}';
const headers = {
  'Content-Type':'application/json',
  'Accept':'application/json'
};

fetch('https://api.kmhfr.health.go.ke/api/facilities/officer_contacts/{id}/',
{
  method: 'PUT',
  body: inputBody,
```
```javascript
  headers: headers
})
.then(function(res) {
    return res.json();
}).then(function(body) {
    console.log(body);
});

```

`GET /api/facilities/officers/`

*Lists and creates officers*

name  -- name of an officer
registration_number -- The official registration  number of an officer
job_title --  A job title's pk
Created --  Date the record was Created
Updated -- Date the record was Updated
Created_by -- User who created the record
Updated_by -- User who updated the record
active  -- Boolean is the record active
deleted -- Boolean is the record deleted

<h3 id="api_facilities_officers_list-parameters">Parameters</h3>

|Name|In|Type|Required|Description|
|---|---|---|---|---|
|ordering|query|string|false|Which field to use when ordering the results.|
|page|query|integer|false|A page number within the paginated result set.|
|page_size|query|integer|false|Number of results to return per page.|

> Example responses

> 200 Response

<BrowserWindow>
```json
{
  "count": 0,
  "next": "http://example.com",
  "previous": "http://example.com",
  "results": [
    {
      "id": "497f6eca-6276-4993-bfeb-53cbbbba6f08",
      "job_title_name": "string",
      "created": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
      "updated": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
      "deleted": true,
      "active": true,
      "search": "string",
      "name": "string",
      "id_number": "string",
      "registration_number": "string",
      "created_by": 0,
      "updated_by": 0,
      "job_title": "07cff277-c099-4115-be2b-d9f439458a4a",
      "contacts": [
        "497f6eca-6276-4993-bfeb-53cbbbba6f08"
      ]
    }
  ]
}
```
</BrowserWindow>



<h3 id="api_facilities_officers_list-responses">Responses</h3>

|Status|Meaning|Description|Schema|
|---|---|---|---|
|200|[OK](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-6.3.1)|none|Inline|

<h3 id="api_facilities_officers_list-responseschema">Response Schema</h3>

Status Code **200**

|Name|Type|Required|Restrictions|Description|
|---|---|---|---|---|
|» count|integer|true|none|none|
|» next|string(uri)¦null|false|none|none|
|» previous|string(uri)¦null|false|none|none|
|» results|[[Officer](schema#officer)]|true|none|none|
|»» id|string(uuid)|false|read-only|none|
|»» job_title_name|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» created|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»» updated|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»» deleted|boolean|false|none|none|
|»» active|boolean|false|none|Indicates whether the record has been retired?|
|»» search|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» name|string|true|none|the name of the officer in-charge e.g Roselyne Wiyanga|
|»» id_number|string¦null|false|none|The  National Identity number of the officer|
|»» registration_number|string¦null|false|none|This is the license number of the officer. e.g for a nurse use the NCK registration number.|
|»» created_by|integer|false|none|none|
|»» updated_by|integer|false|none|none|
|»» job_title|string(uuid)|true|none|none|
|»» contacts|[string]|false|read-only|Personal contacts of the officer in charge|

:::note
To perform this operation, you must be authenticated by means of one of the following methods:
Basic
:::

<h3 id="api_facilities_option_groups_list-responseschema">Response Schema</h3>

Status Code **200**

|Name|Type|Required|Restrictions|Description|
|---|---|---|---|---|
|» count|integer|true|none|none|
|» next|string(uri)¦null|false|none|none|
|» previous|string(uri)¦null|false|none|none|
|» results|[[OptionGroup](schema#optiongroup)]|true|none|none|
|»» id|string(uuid)|false|read-only|none|
|»» options|[[Option](schema#option)]|false|none|none|
|»»» id|string(uuid)|false|read-only|none|
|»»» created|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»»» updated|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»»» deleted|boolean|false|none|none|
|»»» active|boolean|false|none|Indicates whether the record has been retired?|
|»»» search|string|false|read-only|none|
|»»» value|string|true|none|none|
|»»» display_text|string|true|none|none|
|»»» is_exclusive_option|boolean|false|none|none|
|»»» option_type|string|true|none|none|
|»»» created_by|integer|false|none|none|
|»»» updated_by|integer|false|none|none|
|»»» group|string(uuid)|true|none|The option group where the option lies|
|»» created|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»» updated|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»» deleted|boolean|false|none|none|
|»» active|boolean|false|none|Indicates whether the record has been retired?|
|»» search|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» name|string|true|none|none|
|»» created_by|integer|false|none|none|
|»» updated_by|integer|false|none|none|

deleted -- Boolean is the record deleted

|---|---|---|---|---|

|page_size|query|integer|false|Number of results to return per page.|

```json
      "deleted": true,
      "active": true,
      "search": "string",
      "value": "string",

      "group": "fbd899a6-8a66-4f51-a95d-68668de198ae"
    }
  ]
```

|Name|Type|Required|Restrictions|Description|
|---|---|---|---|---|
|» count|integer|true|none|none|
|» next|string(uri)¦null|false|none|none|
|» previous|string(uri)¦null|false|none|none|
|» results|[[Option](schema#option)]|true|none|none|
|»» id|string(uuid)|false|read-only|none|
|»» created|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»» updated|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»» deleted|boolean|false|none|none|
|»» active|boolean|false|none|Indicates whether the record has been retired?|
|»» search|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» value|string|true|none|none|
|»» display_text|string|true|none|none|
|»» is_exclusive_option|boolean|false|none|none|
|»» option_type|string|true|none|none|
|»» created_by|integer|false|none|none|
|»» updated_by|integer|false|none|none|
|»» group|string(uuid)|true|none|The option group where the option lies|

`GET /api/facilities/owners/`

*List and creates a list of owners*

name -- The name of an owner
description -- The description of an owner
abbreviation -- The abbreviation of an owner
code --  The code of an owner
owner_type -- An owner-type's pk
Created --  Date the record was Created
Updated -- Date the record was Updated
Created_by -- User who created the record
Updated_by -- User who updated the record
active  -- Boolean is the record active
deleted -- Boolean is the record deleted

<h3 id="api_facilities_owners_list-parameters">Parameters</h3>

|Name|In|Type|Required|Description|
|---|---|---|---|---|
|ordering|query|string|false|Which field to use when ordering the results.|
|page|query|integer|false|A page number within the paginated result set.|
|page_size|query|integer|false|Number of results to return per page.|

> Example responses

> 200 Response

<BrowserWindow>
```json
{
  "count": 0,
  "next": "http://example.com",
  "previous": "http://example.com",
  "results": [
    {
      "id": "497f6eca-6276-4993-bfeb-53cbbbba6f08",
      "owner_type_name": "string",
      "created": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
      "updated": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
      "deleted": true,
      "active": true,
      "search": "string",
      "name": "string",
      "description": "string",
      "code": "string",
      "abbreviation": "string",
      "created_by": 0,
      "updated_by": 0,
      "owner_type": "2c36d811-befc-4f66-ac99-1f27e70bdb0b"
    }
  ]
}
```
</BrowserWindow>



<h3 id="api_facilities_owners_list-responses">Responses</h3>

|Status|Meaning|Description|Schema|
|---|---|---|---|
|200|[OK](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-6.3.1)|none|Inline|

<h3 id="api_facilities_owners_list-responseschema">Response Schema</h3>

Status Code **200**

|Name|Type|Required|Restrictions|Description|
|---|---|---|---|---|
|» count|integer|true|none|none|
|» next|string(uri)¦null|false|none|none|
|» previous|string(uri)¦null|false|none|none|
|» results|[[Owner](schema#owner)]|true|none|none|
|»» id|string(uuid)|false|read-only|none|
|»» owner_type_name|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» created|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»» updated|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»» deleted|boolean|false|none|none|
|»» active|boolean|false|none|Indicates whether the record has been retired?|
|»» search|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» name|string|true|none|The name of owner e.g Ministry of Health.|
|»» description|string¦null|false|none|A brief summary of the owner.|
|»» code|string|false|read-only|A unique number to identify the owner.Could be up to 7 characters long.|
|»» abbreviation|string¦null|false|none|Short form of the name of the owner e.g Ministry of health could be shortened as MOH|
|»» created_by|integer|false|none|none|
|»» updated_by|integer|false|none|none|
|»» owner_type|string(uuid)|true|none|The classification of the owner e.g INDIVIDUAL|

:::note
To perform this operation, you must be authenticated by means of one of the following methods:
Basic
:::

### api facilities_regulating_bodies_create

```javascript

  "created": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",

}';

  'Content-Type':'application/json',
  'Accept':'application/json'
};
```

|»» id|string(uuid)|false|read-only|none|
|»» contact_text|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» contact_type|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» created|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»» updated|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»» deleted|boolean|false|none|none|
|»» active|boolean|false|none|Indicates whether the record has been retired?|
|»» search|string|false|read-only|none|

`POST /api/facilities/regulation_status/`

*Lists and creates regulation statuses*

name -- name of a regulation status
description -- description of a regulation status
Created --  Date the record was Created
Updated -- Date the record was Updated
Created_by -- User who created the record
Updated_by -- User who updated the record
active  -- Boolean is the record active
deleted -- Boolean is the record deleted

> Body parameter

<BrowserWindow>
```json
{
  "created": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
  "updated": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
  "deleted": true,
  "active": true,
  "name": "string",
  "description": "string",
  "is_initial_state": true,
  "is_final_state": true,
  "is_default": true,
  "created_by": 0,
  "updated_by": 0,

}
```
</BrowserWindow>

<h3 id="api_facilities_regulator_sync_list-responseschema">Response Schema</h3>

Status Code **200**

|Name|Type|Required|Restrictions|Description|
|---|---|---|---|---|
|» count|integer|true|none|none|
|» next|string(uri)¦null|false|none|none|
|» previous|string(uri)¦null|false|none|none|
|» results|[[RegulatorSync](schema#regulatorsync)]|true|none|none|
|»» id|string(uuid)|false|read-only|none|
|»» county_name|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» owner_name|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» facility_type_name|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» regulatory_body_name|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» probable_matches|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» created|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»» updated|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»» deleted|boolean|false|none|none|
|»» active|boolean|false|none|Indicates whether the record has been retired?|
|»» search|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» name|string|true|none|The official name of the facility|
|»» registration_number|string|true|none|The registration number given by the regulator|
|»» county|integer|true|none|The code of the county|
|»» mfl_code|integer¦null|false|read-only|The assigned MFL code|
|»» created_by|integer|false|none|none|
|»» updated_by|integer|false|none|none|
|»» facility_type|string(uuid)|true|none|The type of the facility e.g Medical Clinic|
|»» owner|string(uuid)|true|none|The owner of the facility|
|»» regulatory_body|string(uuid)|false|read-only|The regulatory body the record came from|

:::note
To perform this operation, you must be authenticated by means of one of the following methods:
Basic
:::

|» count|integer|true|none|none|
|» next|string(uri)¦null|false|none|none|
|» previous|string(uri)¦null|false|none|none|
|» results|[[RegulatoryBodyUser](schema#regulatorybodyuser)]|true|none|none|
|»» id|string(uuid)|false|read-only|none|
|»» user_email|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» user_name|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» regulatory_body_name|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» user|integer|false|none|none|
|»» regulatory_body|string(uuid)|false|none|none|
|»» created|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»» updated|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»» deleted|boolean|false|none|none|
|»» active|boolean|false|none|Indicates whether the record has been retired?|
|»» search|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» created_by|integer|false|none|none|
|»» updated_by|integer|false|none|none|

active  -- Boolean is the record active
deleted -- Boolean is the record deleted

|page_size|query|integer|false|Number of results to return per page.|

```json
      "active": true,
      "search": "string",
      "name": "string",
      "description": "string",
      "abbreviation": "string",
```

|» previous|string(uri)¦null|false|none|none|

|»» id|string(uuid)|false|read-only|none|
|»» created|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»» updated|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»» deleted|boolean|false|none|none|
|»» active|boolean|false|none|Indicates whether the record has been retired?|

|»» name|string|true|none|What is the name of the category?|
|»» description|string¦null|false|none|none|
|»» abbreviation|string¦null|false|none|A short form of the category e.g ANC for antenatal|
|»» created_by|integer|false|none|none|
|»» updated_by|integer|false|none|none|

### api facilities_specialities_list



> Code samples

```javascript

const headers = {
  'Accept':'application/json'
};

    return res.json();

    console.log(body);
});

```

`GET /api/facilities/specialities/`

*Lists and creates specialities.*

category -- Speciality category pk
Created --  Date the record was Created
Updated -- Date the record was Updated
Created_by -- User who created the record
Updated_by -- User who updated the record
active  -- Boolean is the record active
deleted -- Boolean is the record deleted

<h3 id="api_facilities_specialities_list-parameters">Parameters</h3>

|Name|In|Type|Required|Description|
|---|---|---|---|---|
|ordering|query|string|false|Which field to use when ordering the results.|
|page|query|integer|false|A page number within the paginated result set.|
|page_size|query|integer|false|Number of results to return per page.|

> Example responses

> 200 Response

<BrowserWindow>
```json
{
  "count": 0,
  "next": "http://example.com",
  "previous": "http://example.com",
  "results": [
    {
      "id": "497f6eca-6276-4993-bfeb-53cbbbba6f08",
      "category_name": "string",
      "created": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
      "updated": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
      "deleted": true,
      "active": true,
      "search": "string",
      "name": "string",
      "description": "string",
      "abbreviation": "string",
      "code": "string",
      "created_by": 0,
      "updated_by": 0,
      "category": "86d23d13-9dbb-46f3-82d0-25253c7750c3"
    }
  ]
}
```
</BrowserWindow>



<h3 id="api_facilities_specialities_list-responses">Responses</h3>

|Status|Meaning|Description|Schema|
|---|---|---|---|
|200|[OK](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-6.3.1)|none|Inline|

<h3 id="api_facilities_specialities_list-responseschema">Response Schema</h3>

Status Code **200**

|Name|Type|Required|Restrictions|Description|
|---|---|---|---|---|
|» count|integer|true|none|none|
|» next|string(uri)¦null|false|none|none|
|» previous|string(uri)¦null|false|none|none|
|» results|[[Speciality](schema#speciality)]|true|none|none|
|»» id|string(uuid)|false|read-only|none|
|»» category_name|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» created|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»» updated|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»» deleted|boolean|false|none|none|
|»» active|boolean|false|none|Indicates whether the record has been retired?|
|»» search|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» name|string|true|none|none|
|»» description|string¦null|false|none|none|
|»» abbreviation|string¦null|false|none|A short form for the speciality|
|»» code|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» created_by|integer|false|none|none|
|»» updated_by|integer|false|none|none|
|»» category|string(uuid)|true|none|The classification that the specialities lies in.|

:::note
To perform this operation, you must be authenticated by means of one of the following methods:
Basic
:::

`GET /api/facilities/speciality_categories/`

*Lists and creates service categories.*

Created ---  Date the record was Created
Updated -- Date the record was Updated
Created_by -- User who created the record
Updated_by -- User who updated the record
active  -- Boolean is the record active
deleted -- Boolean is the record deleted

<h3 id="api_facilities_speciality_categories_list-parameters">Parameters</h3>

|Name|In|Type|Required|Description|
|---|---|---|---|---|
|ordering|query|string|false|Which field to use when ordering the results.|
|page|query|integer|false|A page number within the paginated result set.|
|page_size|query|integer|false|Number of results to return per page.|

> Example responses

> 200 Response

<BrowserWindow>
```json
{
  "count": 0,
  "next": "http://example.com",
  "previous": "http://example.com",
  "results": [
    {
      "id": "497f6eca-6276-4993-bfeb-53cbbbba6f08",
      "created": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
      "updated": "2019-08-24T14:15:22Z",
      "deleted": true,
      "active": true,
      "search": "string",
      "name": "string",
      "description": "string",
      "abbreviation": "string",
      "created_by": 0,
      "updated_by": 0,
      "parent": "42e2bc1b-6741-4e2e-b138-97b4a342c999"
    }
  ]
}
```
</BrowserWindow>



<h3 id="api_facilities_speciality_categories_list-responses">Responses</h3>

|Status|Meaning|Description|Schema|
|---|---|---|---|
|200|[OK](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7231#section-6.3.1)|none|Inline|

<h3 id="api_facilities_speciality_categories_list-responseschema">Response Schema</h3>

Status Code **200**

|Name|Type|Required|Restrictions|Description|
|---|---|---|---|---|
|» count|integer|true|none|none|
|» next|string(uri)¦null|false|none|none|
|» previous|string(uri)¦null|false|none|none|
|» results|[[SpecialityCategory](schema#specialitycategory)]|true|none|none|
|»» id|string(uuid)|false|read-only|none|
|»» created|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»» updated|string(date-time)|false|none|none|
|»» deleted|boolean|false|none|none|
|»» active|boolean|false|none|Indicates whether the record has been retired?|
|»» search|string|false|read-only|none|
|»» name|string|true|none|What is the name of the category?|
|»» description|string¦null|false|none|none|
|»» abbreviation|string¦null|false|none|A short form of the category e.g ANC for antenatal|
|»» created_by|integer|false|none|none|
|»» updated_by|integer|false|none|none|
|»» parent|string(uuid)¦null|false|none|The parent category under which the category falls|

:::note
To perform this operation, you must be authenticated by means of one of the following methods:
Basic
:::
